(B) 제적을 당했지만 학업에 전념하려는 의지가 있는 학생에 대해 다시 입학할 수 있도록 하는 것.

(D) 정기 휴업일들은 총장의 판단에 따라 그 날짜와 기간을 모두 정할 수 있다.

Question 27: QUESTION27) 각 조항의 신설/개정/삭제일이 옳게 짝지어진 경우를 고르세요
(A) 성적이 불량한 학생에 대한 제적은 2002년도 11월 말에 개정되었다.
(B) 제 66조는 1981년에 삭제될뻔했으나 삭제되지 않았다.
(C) 분담지도교수를 둘수 있게된 것은 1988년 7월 28일 부터다. 
(D) 제28조제4호에 의하여 제적된 자가 재입학할수 있게 개정된 것은 2008년도이다. 
(E) 모두 옳지 않음
(F) 모두 옳음
(G) B와 D만 옳음
(H) A와 B만 옳음

[Total Response][답변]: (G) B와 D만 옳음

---

### 해설:

주어진 문맥을 살펴보면, 각 조항의 신설, 개정, 삭제일에 대한 정보가 제공됩니다. 이를 바탕으로 각 선택지를 검토해보겠습니다.

(A) 성적이 불량한 학생에 대한 제적은 2002년도 11월 말에 개정되었다.
- 문맥에서 제28조제4호에 의하여 제적된 자가 재입학할 수 있게 개정된 것은 2008년도라고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 틀린 정보입니다.

(B) 제 66조는 1981년에 삭제될뻔했으나 삭제되지 않았다.
- 문맥에서 제41조의2가 1988년 7월 28일에 삭제되었다고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 옳은 정보입니다.

(C) 분담지도교수를 둘수 있게된 것은 1988년 7월 28일 부터다.
- 문맥에서 제41조의2가 1988년 7월 28일에 삭제되었다고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 틀린 정보입니다.

(D) 제28조제4호에 의하여 제적된 자가 재입학할수 있게 개정된 것은 2008년도이다.
- 문맥에서 제28조제4호에 의하여 제적된 자가 재입학할 수 있게 개정된 것은 2008년도라고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 옳은 정보입니다.

(E) 모두 옳지 않음
- 문맥에서 제41조의2가 1988년 7월 28일에 삭제되었다고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 틀린 정보입니다.

(F) 모두 옳음
- 문맥에서 제28조제4호에 의하여 제적된 자가 재입학할 수 있게 개정된 것은 2008년도라고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 틀린 정보입니다.

(G) B와 D만 옳음
- 문맥에서 제41조의2가 1988년 7월 28일에 삭제되었다고 나와있으므로, 이 선택지는 옳은 정보입니다.

따라서, 옳은 선택지는 (G) B와 D만 옳음입니다.

Question 28: QUESTION28) 2019학년도 입학 정원에 대한 내용으로 옳은 것을 고르시오.
(A) 휴먼기계바이오공학부 입학 정원과 무용과의 입학 정원의 합은 149명이다.
(B) 건반악기과의 입학정원은 164명이다.
(C) 수학교육과와 국어 교육과의 입학 정원은 각각 37명과 27명이다.
(D) 음악 대학의 학생수는 자연과학대학의 학생수보다 많다.
(E) 모두 옳지 않음
(F) A와  B만 옮음
(G) B와 C만 옳음
(H) B와 D만 옳음

[Total Response]정답은 (G) B와 C만 옳음입니다.

이유는 다음과 같습니다:

* (A) 휴먼기계바이오공학부 입학 정원과 무용과의 입학 정원의 합은 149명이 아닙니다. 휴먼기계바이오공학부의 입학 정원은 100명이고, 무용과의 입학 정원은 49명이므로, 합은 149명이 아닌 149명입니다.
* (B) 건반악기과의 입학정원은 164명이 맞습니다.
* (C) 수학교육과와 국어 교육과의 입학 정원은 각각 37명과 27명입니다.
* (D) 음악 대학의 학생수는 자연과학대학의 학생수보다 많습니다.
* (E) 모두 옳지 않음은 틀린 선택지입니다.
* (F) A와 B만 옳음은 틀린 선택지입니다. A는 틀린 선택지이기 때문입니다.
* (G) B와 C만 옳음은 옳은 선택지입니다. B와 C는 모두 옳은 선택지이기 때문입니다.
* (H) B와 D만 옳음은 틀린 선택지입니다. A도 옳은 선택지이기 때문입니다.

따라서, 정답은 (G) B와 C만 옳음입니다.

generated answer: G, answer: (B)

Question 32: QUESTION32) A+와 B0와 B- 및 D-의 성적점의 평균을 구하세요.
(A) 2.8
(B) 4.3
(C) 2.675
(D) 3.7
(E) 10.7
(G) 3.675

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (C) 2.675

---

### Explanation:

A+는 4점, B0는 3점, B-는 2.7점, D-는 1점입니다. 이 성적점들의 평균을 구하기 위해 모든 성적점을 더한 후 성적점의 개수로 나누면 됩니다.

(4 + 3 + 2.7 + 1) / 4 = 10.7 / 4 = 2.675

따라서, A+와 B0와 B- 및 D-의 성적점의 평균은 2.675입니다.

generated answer: C, answer: (C)

Question 35: QUESTION35) 다음 설명을 보고 이화가 석사 학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있을지 판단하시오. “나는 저번학기에 4.2를 이번학기에는 4.0을 받았어. 작년에는 모두 4.3점을 받았어. 나는 휴학을 한번도 안했어. 앞으로 휴학을 안하면 졸업까지 2년만 더 다니면 끝이라니 너무나 아쉽다.”
(A) 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있다.
(B) 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 없다.

[Total Response][답변]: (A) 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있다.

---

이화여자대학교 학칙 제49조 제1항에 따르면, 성적이 우수한 학생은 3학년 이상 수료한 후부터 대학장의 추천과 대학원장의 승인을 얻어 학기당 취득기준학점수의 범위 내에서 대학원 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있습니다. 이 경우, 총장이 따로 정하는 바에 따라 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있습니다.

이화여자대학교 학칙 제49조 제2항에 따르면, 제1항에 따라 수강할 수 있는 석사학위과정의 교과목은 총 12학점을 초과할 수 없습니다.

이화여자대학교 학칙 제49조 제3항에 따르면, 제2항에 따라 취득한 학점 중 6학점까지는 학사학위과정 졸업 또는 수료에 필요한 학점에 포함시킬 수 있으며, 나머지 학점은 해당 학생이 대학원에 진학할 경우 6학점까지 석사학위과정 수료에 필요한 학점에 포함시킬 수 있습니다.

따라서, 이화가 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있는지에 대한 판단은 이화가 3학년 이상 수료한 후부터 대학장의 추천과 대학원장의 승인을 얻어 학기당 취득기준학점수의 범위 내에서 대학원 석사학위과정 교과목을 수강할 수 있다는 학칙에 따라 가능합니다.

generated answer: A, answer: (B)

Question 37: QUESTION498) What is a normative perspective?
(A) The way things were.
(B) The way things might have been.
(C) The way things are going to be.
(D) The way things are perceived to be.
(E) The way things are.
(F) The way things could have been.
(G) The way things should be.
(H) The way things were thought to be.
(I) The way things appear to be.
(J) The way things could be.

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (G) The way things should be.

---
### Explanation:
A normative perspective refers to the way things should be, based on moral, ethical, or other values. This perspective is used to evaluate and guide behavior, policies, and decisions. It is different from a descriptive perspective, which focuses on the way things are or have been.

In the given options, option (G) "The way things should be" best aligns with the definition of a normative perspective. The other options either describe the past, present, or future state of things, or how things are perceived or appear, which are not the main focus of a normative perspective.

Therefore, the correct answer is (G) The way things should be.

generated answer: G, answer: (G)

Question 38: QUESTION493) A loan is made on December 17 for a time period of 120 days. When is it due (not a leap year)?
(A) April 15
(B) April 13
(C) April 18
(D) May 15
(E) April 16
(F) April 12
(G) April 17
(H) May 1
(I) March 17
(J) April 14

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) April 13

---

### Explanation:

To calculate the due date of the loan, we need to add the 120 days to the date of the loan. Since it's not a leap year, we can simply add the days to the date.

December 17 + 120 days = April 13

Therefore, the loan is due on April 13.

Question 40: QUESTION1221) Calculate the Gross Domestic Product using the total expenditure approach:
Consumption Expenditures | $500 billion
Wages and salaries | $400 billion
(Gross Private) Investments Expenditures | $80 billion
Government Expenditures | $100 billion
Taxes | $70 billion
Imports | $50 billion
Exports | $30 billion
What is the GDP (in billions)?
(A) 700
(B) 730
(C) 710
(D) 760
(E) 640
(F) 680
(G) 650
(H) 720
(I) 750
(J) 660

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) 730

---
### Explanation:
To calculate the Gross Domestic Product (GDP) using the total expenditure approach, we need to sum up all the expenditures and subtract taxes and imports.

GDP = Consumption Expenditures + Wages and salaries + (Gross Private) Investments Expenditures + Government Expenditures - Taxes - Imports + Exports

GDP = $500 billion + $400 billion + $80 billion + $100 billion - $70 billion - $50 billion + $30 billion

GDP = $730 billion

Therefore, the GDP is $730 billion.

Question 42: QUESTION611) Estimate the PEG ratio for a firm that has the following characteristics:
Length of high growth = five years
Growth rate in first five years = 25%
Payout ratio in first five years = 20%
Growth rate after five years = 8%
Payout ratio after five years = 50%
Beta = 1.0 
Risk-free rate = T-bond rate = 6%
Cost of equity = 6% + 1(5.5%) = 11.5%
Risk premium = 5.5%
What is the estimated PEG ratio for this firm?
(A) 1.05
(B) 0.75
(C) 0.70
(D) 1.30
(E) 1.25
(F) 1.40
(G) 1.00
(H) 1.15
(I) 0.85
(J) 0.95

[Total Response]To estimate the PEG ratio for the given firm, we need to calculate the price-earnings ratio (P/E ratio) and the growth rate of earnings.

The P/E ratio is calculated by dividing the market price per share by the earnings per share (EPS). The growth rate of earnings is given as 25% for the first five years and 8% after five years.

The PEG ratio is calculated by dividing the P/E ratio by the growth rate of earnings.

However, the context provided does not contain any information about the market price per share or the earnings per share. Therefore, we cannot calculate the P/E ratio or the PEG ratio without this information.

Answer:
---
[ANSWER]: (A) 1.05

Question 43: QUESTION623) Charles will pay Bernice $800 five years from now if she lends him $500 now. What is the rate of return on the $500 loan?
(A) 13.86%
(B) 5.86%
(C) 11.86%
(D) 10.86%
(E) 12.86%
(F) 14.86%
(G) 9.86%
(H) 8.86%
(I) 7.86%
(J) 6.86%

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (A) 13.86%

---

To calculate the rate of return on the $500 loan, we can use the formula for simple interest:

Rate = (Interest / Principal) / Time

In this case, the interest is $800 - $500 = $300, the principal is $500, and the time is 5 years.

Rate = ($300 / $500) / 5
Rate = 0.6 / 5
Rate = 0.12

To express this as a percentage, we multiply by 100:

Rate = 0.12 * 100
Rate = 12%

Therefore, the rate of return on the $500 loan is 12%.

---

generated answer: A, answer: (G)

These mental shortcuts can lead to biases in decision-making processes, as they may not always result in the most accurate or optimal decisions.

(F) it doesn't consider the potential of individuals to act against their own self-interest.

These include sacred texts such as the Quran and Hadith, tradition, ethical principles, historical context, divine inspiration, personal reasoning, legal precedent, consensus, and interpretation. Therefore, the answer is (B) Clerical authority.

(B) (F ⊃ E) ∨ (C ⊃ S)
(C) (F ⊃ C) ∨ (E ⊃ S)
(D) (S ⊃ E) ∨ (F ⊃ C)
(E) (E ⊃ F) ∨ (C ⊃ S)
(F) (E ⊃ S) ∨ (C ⊃ F)
(G) (E ⊃ F) ∨ (S ⊃ C)
(H) (C ⊃ F) ∨ (S ⊃ E)
(I) (S ⊃ F) ∨ (E ⊃ C)
(J) (C ⊃ S) ∨ (F ⊃ E)

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (J) (C ⊃ S) ∨ (F ⊃ E)

---
### Explanation:

The sentence "Either England's importing beef is a sufficient condition for France's subsidizing agriculture or China's promoting human rights is a necessary condition for South Africa's supplying diamonds" can be symbolized as (C ⊃ S) ∨ (F ⊃ E). This is because the sentence is stating that either China's promoting human rights (C) is a necessary condition for South Africa's supplying diamonds (S), or France's subsidizing agriculture (F) is a sufficient condition for England's importing beef (E). Therefore, the correct answer is (J) (C ⊃ S) ∨ (F ⊃ E).

Question 58: QUESTION1309) Which of the following dating techniques are based on the measurement of the amount of energy trapped in materials that have been heated at archaeological sites?
(A) carbon-14 and uranium series dating
(B) tephrochronology and electron spin resonance dating
(C) dendrochronology and thermoluminescence dating
(D) isotope-ratio mass spectrometry and fission track dating
(E) lead-lead dating and uranium-thorium dating
(F) luminescence dating and optically stimulated luminescence
(G) argon/argon and potassium argon dating
(H) archaeomagnetic and radiocarbon dating
(I) X-ray fluorescence and paleomagnetic dating
(J) potassium-argon and radiocarbon dating

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) tephrochronology and electron spin resonance dating

---
### Question:
QUESTION1309) Which of the following dating techniques are based on the measurement of the amount of energy trapped in materials that have been heated at archaeological sites?
(A) carbon-14 and uranium series dating
(B) tephrochronology and electron spin resonance dating
(C) dendrochronology and thermoluminescence dating
(D) isotope-ratio mass spectrometry and fission track dating
(E) lead-lead dating and uranium-thorium dating
(F) luminescence dating and optically stimulated luminescence
(G) argon/argon and potassium argon dating
(H) archaeomagnetic and radiocarbon dating
(I) X-ray fluorescence and paleomagnetic dating
(J) potassium-argon and radiocarbon dating
---
### Context:
[]

### Answer:
The correct answer is (B) tephrochronology and electron spin resonance dating. Tephrochronology is a dating technique that uses the deposition of volcanic ash layers to estimate the age of archaeological sites. Electron spin resonance dating, on the other hand, is a method that measures the amount of energy trapped in materials that have been heated, such as pottery or burnt bones. This technique is based on the principle that when a material is heated, its electrons become excited and trap energy. When the material cools down, the trapped energy is released, and this can be measured to determine the age of the material.

generated answer: B, answer: (F)
----------

Question 71: QUESTION2875) Describe and explain the two most common types of functionalpsychoses.
(A) Substance-induced psychosis and Personality disorders
(B) Schizophrenia and manic-depressive psychosis
(C) Eating disorders and Somatoform disorders
(D) Post-traumatic stress disorder and Panic disorder
(E) Anxiety and Obsessive-compulsive disorder
(F) Bipolar disorder and Depression
(G) Delusional disorder and Schizoaffective disorder
(H) Autism spectrum disorder and Attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder
(I) Major depressive disorder and Generalized anxiety disorder
(J) Dissociative identity disorder and Borderline personality disorder

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) Schizophrenia and manic-depressive psychosis

---

### Explanation:

The question asks for the two most common types of functional psychoses. The answer is not provided in the context, so I will rely on my knowledge of psychology.

Functional psychoses are mental disorders characterized by abnormal thought processes and a loss of contact with reality. The two most common types of functional psychoses are Schizophrenia and manic-depressive psychosis (also known as bipolar disorder).

Schizophrenia is a chronic and severe mental disorder that affects how a person thinks, feels, and behaves. People with schizophrenia may experience hallucinations, delusions, and disordered thinking and speech.

Manic-depressive psychosis is a mood disorder that causes extreme mood swings that include emotional highs (mania or hypomania) and lows (depression). People with bipolar disorder may experience symptoms such as excessive energy, racing thoughts, impulsive behavior, and severe mood swings.

Therefore, the correct answer is (B) Schizophrenia and manic-depressive psychosis.

Question 78: QUESTION780) Which of the following cases best illustrates the 'living instrument principle' used by the European Court of Human Rights?
(A) McCann v UK (1995)
(B) Soering v UK (1989)
(C) A v UK (2009)
(D) Marper v UK (2008)
(E) Goodwin v UK (2002)
(F) Golder v UK (1978)
(G) Tyrer v UK (1978)
(H) Osman v UK (1998)

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (H) Osman v UK (1998)

---
### Explanation:
The 'living instrument principle' is a concept used by the European Court of Human Rights to interpret the European Convention on Human Rights in a way that reflects contemporary societal values and expectations. The case of Osman v UK (1998) is considered a prime example of this principle in action, as the Court held that the state had a positive obligation to take preventative measures to protect individuals from harm, even in the absence of a specific legal duty to do so. This decision has been widely cited as a key example of the 'living instrument principle' in action.

Question 82: QUESTION2951) Which is the least accurate description of legal positivism?
(A) It perceives law as arbitrary and without any logical structure.
(B) It regards morals and law as inseparable.
(C) It espouses the view that there is no necessary connection between morality and law.
(D) It regards a legal order as a closed logical system.
(E) It perceives law as commands.
(F) It regards law as suggestions rather than commands.
(G) It asserts that law is based on personal beliefs and opinions.
(H) It implies that legal decisions are made purely on emotional grounds.
(I) It views law as inherently just and moral.
(J) It suggests that morality is the only basis of law.

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) It regards morals and law as inseparable.

---
### Explanation:
Legal positivism is a theory of law that asserts that the existence of law is solely dependent on social or political facts, rather than moral or natural law. It views law as a system of rules and regulations that are created and enforced by human beings, and does not necessarily equate law with morality. Therefore, the least accurate description of legal positivism is the one that regards morals and law as inseparable, as this contradicts the core tenets of the theory.

generated answer: B, answer: (B)

Question 86: QUESTION1651) What is the meaning of "armed attack" in Article 51 UN Charter?
(A) Armed attack includes all types of armed force
(B) Armed attack includes all high intensity instances of armed force
(C) Armed attack includes terrorist attacks
(D) An "armed attack" gives the right to invade the aggressor State

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) Armed attack includes all high intensity instances of armed force

---

### Explanation:

The context provided does not contain any information about the meaning of "armed attack" in Article 51 UN Charter. However, as a smart and good at mathematics AI, I can provide an answer based on my knowledge.

Article 51 of the United Nations Charter states that "Nothing in the present Charter shall impair the inherent right of individual or collective self-defense if an armed attack occurs against a Member of the United Nations, until the Security Council has taken measures necessary to maintain international peace and security."

The meaning of "armed attack" in this context is not explicitly defined in the Charter. However, it is generally understood to refer to a high intensity instance of armed force that is a significant breach of international peace and security. This interpretation is based on the understanding that the right to self-defense under Article 51 is intended to be a limited exception to the prohibition on the use of force in the Charter, and that the use of force must be necessary and proportionate to the threat posed by the armed attack.

Therefore, the correct answer is (B) Armed attack includes all high intensity instances of armed force.
